         <h2 class="styles_Card__Title__vp17Z styles_Card__Title--Is-Serif__2ClLt">
          <a class="styles_Card__TitleLink__1wfDO" href="/us/across-america/80s-themed-vax-thon-inoculates-7-000-u-s-coronavirus-blog" title="'80s-Themed 'Vax-A-Thon' Inoculates 7,000: U.S. Coronavirus Blog">
           '80s-Themed 'Vax-A-Thon' Inoculates 7,000: U.S. Coronavirus Blog
          </a>
         </h2>
         <p class="styles_Card__Description__3tUgd">
          Vaccinated people don't have to wear masks, CDC says; states continue easing restrictions; kids burn masks outside Idaho state capitol.
         </p>
         <div class="styles_Card__BylineWrapper__o7ouG">
          <img alt="Tim Moran's profile picture" class="avatar-img avatar-img--xxs is-lazy-loaded" src="https://patch.com/img/cdn/assets/layout/patch_white_bg.jpg?width=1"/>
          <noscript>

           </noscript>
          </span>
         </div>
        </div>
        <a class="styles_Card__Thumbnail__1-_Rw" href="/us/across-america/80s-themed-vax-thon-inoculates-7-000-u-s-coronavirus-blog" title="'80s-Themed 'Vax-A-Thon' Inoculates 7,000: U.S. Coronavirus Blog">

          Hundreds of bills in state legislatures would restrict or expand voter access ahead of Supreme Court ruling that may gut Voting Rights Act.
